# Awesome Python  

[![Awesome](https://awesome.re/badge.svg)](https://awesome.re)  ![Last commit](https://img.shields.io/github/last-commit/dylanhogg/awesome-python)  [![License: MIT](https://img.shields.io/badge/license-MIT-green.svg)](https://opensource.org/licenses/MIT)  

Hand-picked awesome Python libraries and frameworks, organised by category 🐍  

Interactive version: [www.awesomepython.org](https://www.awesomepython.org/)  
  
<img src='https://www.awesomepython.org/img/media/github-repo-banner.jpg' />  

Updated 01 Jul 2026 with 1,479 repos

## Categories

- [Newly Created Repositories](#newly-created-repositories) - Awesome Python is regularly updated, and this category lists the most recently created GitHub repositories from all the other repositories here (10 repos)
- [Agentic AI](#agentic-ai) - Agentic AI libraries, frameworks and tools: AI agents, workflows, autonomous decision-making, goal-oriented tasks, and API integrations (143 repos)
- [Code Quality](#code-quality) - Code quality tooling: linters, formatters, pre-commit hooks, unused code removal (13 repos)
- [Crypto and Blockchain](#crypto-and-blockchain) - Cryptocurrency and blockchain libraries: trading bots, API integration, Ethereum virtual machine, solidity (8 repos)
- [Data](#data) - General data libraries: data processing, serialisation, formats, databases, SQL, connectors, web crawlers, data generation/augmentation/checks (75 repos)
- [Debugging](#debugging) - Debugging and tracing tools (3 repos)
- [Diffusion Text to Image](#diffusion-text-to-image) - Text-to-image diffusion model libraries, tools and apps for generating images from natural language (38 repos)
- [Finance](#finance) - Financial and quantitative libraries: investment research tools, market data, algorithmic trading, backtesting, financial derivatives (24 repos)
- [Game Development](#game-development) - Game development tools, engines and libraries (4 repos)
- [GIS](#gis) - Geospatial libraries: raster and vector data formats, interactive mapping and visualisation, computing frameworks for processing images, projections (16 repos)
- [Graph](#graph) - Graphs and network libraries: network analysis, graph machine learning, visualisation (3 repos)
- [GUI](#gui) - Graphical user interface libraries and toolkits (6 repos)
- [Jupyter](#jupyter) - Jupyter and JupyterLab and Notebook tools, libraries and plugins (15 repos)
- [LLMs and ChatGPT](#llms-and-chatgpt) - Large language model and GPT libraries and frameworks: auto-gpt, agents, QnA, chain-of-thought workflows, API integations. Also see the <a href="https://github.com/dylanhogg/awesome-python#natural-language-processing">Natural Language Processing</a> category for crossover (342 repos)
- [Math and Science](#math-and-science) - Mathematical, numerical and scientific libraries (21 repos)
- [Machine Learning - General](#machine-learning---general) - General and classical machine learning libraries. See below for other sections covering specialised ML areas (132 repos)
- [Machine Learning - Deep Learning](#machine-learning---deep-learning) - Machine learning libraries that cross over with deep learning in some way (61 repos)
- [Machine Learning - Interpretability](#machine-learning---interpretability) - Machine learning interpretability libraries. Covers explainability, prediction explainations, dashboards, understanding knowledge development in training (15 repos)
- [Machine Learning - Ops](#machine-learning---ops) - MLOps tools, frameworks and libraries: intersection of machine learning, data engineering and DevOps; deployment, health, diagnostics and governance of ML models (47 repos)
- [Machine Learning - Reinforcement](#machine-learning---reinforcement) - Machine learning libraries and toolkits that cross over with reinforcement learning in some way: agent reinforcement learning, agent environemnts, RLHF (21 repos)
- [Machine Learning - Time Series](#machine-learning---time-series) - Machine learning and classical timeseries libraries: forecasting, seasonality, anomaly detection, econometrics (15 repos)
- [Natural Language Processing](#natural-language-processing) - Natural language processing libraries and toolkits: text processing, topic modelling, tokenisers, chatbots. Also see the <a href="https://github.com/dylanhogg/awesome-python#llms-and-chatgpt">LLMs and ChatGPT</a> category for crossover (68 repos)
- [Packaging](#packaging) - Python packaging, dependency management and bundling (18 repos)
- [Pandas](#pandas) - Pandas and dataframe libraries: data analysis, statistical reporting, pandas GUIs, pandas performance optimisations (16 repos)
- [Performance](#performance) - Performance, parallelisation and low level libraries (17 repos)
- [Profiling](#profiling) - Memory and CPU/GPU profiling tools and libraries (7 repos)
- [Security](#security) - Security related libraries: vulnerability discovery, SQL injection, environment auditing (19 repos)
- [Simulation](#simulation) - Simulation libraries: robotics, economic, agent-based, traffic, physics, astronomy, chemistry, quantum simulation. Also see the <a href="https://github.com/dylanhogg/awesome-python#math-and-science">Maths and Science</a> category for crossover (29 repos)
- [Study](#study) - Miscellaneous study resources: algorithms, general resources, system design, code repos for textbooks, best practices, tutorials (58 repos)
- [Template](#template) - Template tools and libraries: cookiecutter repos, generators, quick-starts (9 repos)
- [Terminal](#terminal) - Terminal and console tools and libraries: CLI tools, terminal based formatters, progress bars (15 repos)
- [Testing](#testing) - Testing libraries: unit testing, load testing, acceptance testing, code coverage, browser automation, plugins (10 repos)
- [Typing](#typing) - Typing libraries: static and run-time type checking, annotations (13 repos)
- [Utility](#utility) - General utility libraries: miscellaneous tools, linters, code formatters, version management, package tools, documentation tools (121 repos)
- [Vizualisation](#vizualisation) - Vizualisation tools and libraries. Application frameworks, 2D/3D plotting, dashboards, WebGL (28 repos)
- [Web](#web) - Web related frameworks and libraries: webapp servers, WSGI, ASGI, asyncio, HTTP, REST, user management (39 repos)


## Newly Created Repositories

Awesome Python is regularly updated, and this category lists the most recently created GitHub repositories from all the other repositories here.  

1. <a href="https://github.com/omnigent-ai/omnigent">omnigent-ai/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/omnigent-ai/omnigent">omnigent</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/omnigent-ai/omnigent?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/omnigent-ai/omnigent/stargazers)    
   Omnigent is an open-source AI agent framework and meta-harness: orchestrate Claude Code, Codex, Cursor, Pi, and custom agents — swap harnesses without rewriting, enforce policies and sandboxing, and collaborate in real time from any device.  
   🔗 [omnigent.ai](https://omnigent.ai)  

2. <a href="https://github.com/startrail-org/pixelrag">startrail-org/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/startrail-org/pixelrag">PixelRAG</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/startrail-org/PixelRAG?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/startrail-org/PixelRAG/stargazers)    
   Renders documents as screenshots and retrieves over the images directly.  
   🔗 [pixelrag.ai](https://pixelrag.ai/)  

3. <a href="https://github.com/strukto-ai/mirage">strukto-ai/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/strukto-ai/mirage">mirage</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/strukto-ai/mirage?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/strukto-ai/mirage/stargazers)    
   A Unified Virtual Filesystem For AI Agents  
   🔗 [www.strukto.ai/mirage](https://www.strukto.ai/mirage)  

4. <a href="https://github.com/nutlope/hallmark">nutlope/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/nutlope/hallmark">hallmark</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nutlope/hallmark?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/nutlope/hallmark/stargazers)    
   A design skill for Claude Code, Cursor, and Codex that refuses to look AI-generated.  
   🔗 [www.usehallmark.com](https://www.usehallmark.com/)  

5. <a href="https://github.com/deeplethe/forkd">deeplethe/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/deeplethe/forkd">forkd</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/deeplethe/forkd?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/deeplethe/forkd/stargazers)    
   Fork() for AI agent microVMs. Spawn 100 children in ~100ms from a warm parent; BRANCH a live VM in ~150ms. KVM-isolated, snapshot CoW.  

6. <a href="https://github.com/apple/coreai-models">apple/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/apple/coreai-models">coreai-models</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/apple/coreai-models?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/apple/coreai-models/stargazers)    
   Model export recipes, Python primitives, and Swift runtime utilities for on-device AI  

7. <a href="https://github.com/kitft/natural_language_autoencoders">kitft/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/kitft/natural_language_autoencoders">natural_language_autoencoders</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kitft/natural_language_autoencoders?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/kitft/natural_language_autoencoders/stargazers)    
   Natural Language Autoencoders Produce Unsupervised Explanations of LLM Activations  

8. <a href="https://github.com/facebookresearch/programbench">facebookresearch/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/facebookresearch/programbench">ProgramBench</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebookresearch/ProgramBench?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/facebookresearch/ProgramBench/stargazers)    
   Can Language Models Rebuild Programs From Scratch?  
   🔗 [programbench.com](https://programbench.com)  

9. <a href="https://github.com/hanxiao/knowledge-graph-extractor">hanxiao/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/hanxiao/knowledge-graph-extractor">knowledge-graph-extractor</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hanxiao/knowledge-graph-extractor?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/hanxiao/knowledge-graph-extractor/stargazers)    
   Turn any document or a whole zip into an interactive knowledge graph, using a self-hosted Qwen3.6-35B-A3B-MTP on a single NVIDIA L4  
   🔗 [hanxiao.io/knowledge-graph](https://hanxiao.io/knowledge-graph)  

10. <a href="https://github.com/pythagoras-lm/pythagoras-prover">pythagoras-lm/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/pythagoras-lm/pythagoras-prover">Pythagoras-Prover</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pythagoras-lm/Pythagoras-Prover?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/pythagoras-lm/Pythagoras-Prover/stargazers)

## Agentic AI

Agentic AI libraries, frameworks and tools: AI agents, workflows, autonomous decision-making, goal-oriented tasks, and API integrations.

## Machine Learning - Interpretability

Machine learning interpretability libraries. Covers explainability, prediction explainations, dashboards, understanding knowledge development in training.  

1. <a href="https://github.com/slundberg/shap">slundberg/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/slundberg/shap">shap</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/slundberg/shap?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/slundberg/shap/stargazers)    
   A game theoretic approach to explain the output of any machine learning model.  
   🔗 [shap.readthedocs.io](https://shap.readthedocs.io)  

2. <a href="https://github.com/marcotcr/lime">marcotcr/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/marcotcr/lime">lime</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marcotcr/lime?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/marcotcr/lime/stargazers)    
   Lime: Explaining the predictions of any machine learning classifier  

3. <a href="https://github.com/arize-ai/phoenix">arize-ai/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/arize-ai/phoenix">phoenix</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arize-ai/phoenix?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/arize-ai/phoenix/stargazers)    
   AI Observability & Evaluation  
   🔗 [arize.com/docs/phoenix](https://arize.com/docs/phoenix)  

4. <a href="https://github.com/interpretml/interpret">interpretml/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/interpretml/interpret">interpret</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/interpretml/interpret?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/interpretml/interpret/stargazers)    
   Fit interpretable models. Explain blackbox machine learning.   
   🔗 [interpret.ml/docs](https://interpret.ml/docs)  

5. <a href="https://github.com/pytorch/captum">pytorch/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/pytorch/captum">captum</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pytorch/captum?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/pytorch/captum/stargazers)    
   Model interpretability and understanding for PyTorch  
   🔗 [captum.ai](https://captum.ai)  

6. <a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/lucid">tensorflow/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/lucid">lucid</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tensorflow/lucid?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/tensorflow/lucid/stargazers)    
   A collection of infrastructure and tools for research in neural network interpretability.  

7. <a href="https://github.com/pair-code/lit">pair-code/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/pair-code/lit">lit</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pair-code/lit?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/pair-code/lit/stargazers)    
   The Learning Interpretability Tool: Interactively analyze ML models to understand their behavior in an extensible and framework agnostic interface.  
   🔗 [pair-code.github.io/lit](https://pair-code.github.io/lit)  

8. <a href="https://github.com/maif/shapash">maif/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/maif/shapash">shapash</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/maif/shapash?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/maif/shapash/stargazers)    
   🔅 Shapash: User-friendly Explainability and Interpretability to Develop Reliable and Transparent Machine Learning Models  
   🔗 [maif.github.io/shapash](https://maif.github.io/shapash/)  

9. <a href="https://github.com/transformerlensorg/transformerlens">transformerlensorg/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/transformerlensorg/transformerlens">TransformerLens</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/transformerlensorg/TransformerLens?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/transformerlensorg/TransformerLens/stargazers)    
   A library for mechanistic interpretability of GPT-style language models  
   🔗 [transformerlensorg.github.io/transformerlens](https://transformerlensorg.github.io/TransformerLens/)  

10. <a href="https://github.com/eleutherai/pythia">eleutherai/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/eleutherai/pythia">pythia</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eleutherai/pythia?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/eleutherai/pythia/stargazers)    
   Interpretability analysis and scaling laws to understand how knowledge develops and evolves during training in autoregressive transformers  

11. <a href="https://github.com/google-deepmind/penzai">google-deepmind/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/google-deepmind/penzai">penzai</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google-deepmind/penzai?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/google-deepmind/penzai/stargazers)    
   A JAX library for writing models as legible, functional pytree data structures, along with tools for visualizing, modifying, and analyzing them. Penzai focuses on making it easy to do stuff with models after they have been trained  
   🔗 [penzai.readthedocs.io](https://penzai.readthedocs.io/)  

12. <a href="https://github.com/stanfordnlp/pyreft">stanfordnlp/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/stanfordnlp/pyreft">pyreft</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stanfordnlp/pyreft?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/stanfordnlp/pyreft/stargazers)    
   Stanford NLP Python library for Representation Finetuning (ReFT)  
   🔗 [arxiv.org/abs/2404.03592](https://arxiv.org/abs/2404.03592)  

13. <a href="https://github.com/ethicalml/xai">ethicalml/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/ethicalml/xai">xai</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ethicalml/xai?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/ethicalml/xai/stargazers)    
   XAI is a Machine Learning library that is designed with AI explainability in its core. XAI contains various tools that enable for analysis and evaluation of data and models  
   🔗 [ethical.institute/principles.html#commitment-3](https://ethical.institute/principles.html#commitment-3)  

14. <a href="https://github.com/jbloomaus/saelens">jbloomaus/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/jbloomaus/saelens">SAELens</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jbloomaus/SAELens?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/jbloomaus/SAELens/stargazers)    
   Training Sparse Autoencoders on LLms. Analyse sparse autoencoders and neural network internals.  
   🔗 [decoderesearch.github.io/saelens](https://decoderesearch.github.io/SAELens/)

## Machine Learning - Reinforcement

Machine learning libraries and toolkits that cross over with reinforcement learning in some way: agent reinforcement learning, agent environemnts, RLHF  

1. <a href="https://github.com/openai/gym">openai/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/openai/gym">gym</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openai/gym?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/openai/gym/stargazers)

## Natural Language Processing

Natural language processing libraries and toolkits: text processing, topic modelling, tokenisers, chatbots. Also see the <a href="https://github.com/dylanhogg/awesome-python#llms-and-chatgpt">LLMs and ChatGPT</a> category for crossover.  

1. <a href="https://github.com/huggingface/transformers">huggingface/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/huggingface/transformers">transformers</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/huggingface/transformers?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/huggingface/transformers/stargazers)    
   🤗 Transformers: the model-definition framework for state-of-the-art machine learning models in text, vision, audio, and multimodal models, for both inference and training.   
   🔗 [huggingface.co/transformers](https://huggingface.co/transformers)  

2. <a href="https://github.com/myshell-ai/openvoice">myshell-ai/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/myshell-ai/openvoice">OpenVoice</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/myshell-ai/OpenVoice?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/myshell-ai/OpenVoice/stargazers)    
   Instant voice cloning by MIT and MyShell. Audio foundation model.  
   🔗 [research.myshell.ai/open-voice](https://research.myshell.ai/open-voice)  

3. <a href="https://github.com/explosion/spacy">explosion/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/explosion/spacy">spaCy</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/explosion/spaCy?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/explosion/spaCy/stargazers)

   🔗 [spacy.io](https://spacy.io)  

4. <a href="https://github.com/pytorch/fairseq">pytorch/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/pytorch/fairseq">fairseq</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pytorch/fairseq?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/pytorch/fairseq/stargazers)

5. <a href="https://github.com/vikparuchuri/marker">vikparuchuri/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/vikparuchuri/marker">marker</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vikparuchuri/marker?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/vikparuchuri/marker/stargazers)    
   Marker converts PDF, EPUB, and MOBI to markdown. It's 10x faster than nougat, more accurate on most documents, and has low hallucination risk.  
   🔗 [www.datalab.to](https://www.datalab.to)

1. <a href="https://github.com/astral-sh/uv">astral-sh/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/astral-sh/uv">uv</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/astral-sh/uv?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/astral-sh/uv/stargazers)

   Automatic SQL injection and database takeover tool  
   🔗 [sqlmap.org](http://sqlmap.org)  

3. <a href="https://github.com/certbot/certbot">certbot/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/certbot/certbot">certbot</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/certbot/certbot?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/certbot/certbot/stargazers)    
   Certbot is EFF's tool to obtain certs from Let's Encrypt and (optionally) auto-enable HTTPS on your server.  It can also act as a client for any other CA that uses the ACME protocol.  

4. <a href="https://github.com/aquasecurity/trivy">aquasecurity/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/aquasecurity/trivy">trivy</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aquasecurity/trivy?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/aquasecurity/trivy/stargazers)    
   Find vulnerabilities, misconfigurations, secrets, SBOM in containers, Kubernetes, code repositories, clouds and more  
   🔗 [trivy.dev](https://trivy.dev)  

5. <a href="https://github.com/alibaba/opensandbox">alibaba/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/alibaba/opensandbox">OpenSandbox</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alibaba/OpenSandbox?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/alibaba/OpenSandbox/stargazers)    
   Secure, Fast, and Extensible Sandbox runtime for AI agents.  
   🔗 [open-sandbox.ai](https://open-sandbox.ai)  

6. <a href="https://github.com/nvidia/skillspector">nvidia/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/nvidia/skillspector">SkillSpector</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nvidia/SkillSpector?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/nvidia/SkillSpector/stargazers)    
   Security scanner for AI agent skills. Detect vulnerabilities, malicious patterns, and security risks.  

7. <a href="https://github.com/bridgecrewio/checkov">bridgecrewio/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/bridgecrewio/checkov">checkov</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bridgecrewio/checkov?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/bridgecrewio/checkov/stargazers)    
   Checkov is a static code analysis tool for infrastructure as code (IaC) and also a software composition analysis (SCA) tool for images and open source packages.  
   🔗 [www.checkov.io](https://www.checkov.io/)

## Machine Learning - Time Series

Machine learning and classical timeseries libraries: forecasting, seasonality, anomaly detection, econometrics.  

1. <a href="https://github.com/facebook/prophet">facebook/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/facebook/prophet">prophet</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebook/prophet?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/facebook/prophet/stargazers)    
   Tool for producing high quality forecasts for time series data that has multiple seasonality with linear or non-linear growth.  
   🔗 [facebook.github.io/prophet](https://facebook.github.io/prophet)  

2. <a href="https://github.com/sktime/sktime">sktime/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/sktime/sktime">sktime</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sktime/sktime?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/sktime/sktime/stargazers)    
   A unified framework for machine learning with time series  
   🔗 [www.sktime.net](https://www.sktime.net)  

3. <a href="https://github.com/unit8co/darts">unit8co/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/unit8co/darts">darts</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/unit8co/darts?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/unit8co/darts/stargazers)    
   A python library for user-friendly forecasting and anomaly detection on time series.  
   🔗 [unit8co.github.io/darts](https://unit8co.github.io/darts/)

   Automatic extraction of relevant features from time series:  
   🔗 [tsfresh.readthedocs.io](http://tsfresh.readthedocs.io)  

5. <a href="https://github.com/google-research/timesfm">google-research/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/google-research/timesfm">timesfm</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google-research/timesfm?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/google-research/timesfm/stargazers)    
   TimesFM (Time Series Foundation Model) is a pretrained time-series foundation model developed by Google Research for time-series forecasting.  
   🔗 [research.google/blog/a-decoder-only-foundation-model-for-time-series-forecasting](https://research.google/blog/a-decoder-only-foundation-model-for-time-series-forecasting/)  

6. <a href="https://github.com/facebookresearch/kats">facebookresearch/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/facebookresearch/kats">Kats</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/facebookresearch/Kats?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/facebookresearch/Kats/stargazers)    
   Kats, a kit to analyze time series data, a lightweight, easy-to-use, generalizable, and extendable framework to perform time series analysis, from understanding the key statistics and characteristics, detecting change points and anomalies, to forecasting future trends.   

7. <a href="https://github.com/awslabs/gluonts">awslabs/</a><b><a href="https://github.com/awslabs/gluonts">gluonts</a></b> [![Stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/awslabs/gluonts?style=flat-square&logo=github)](https://github.com/awslabs/gluonts/stargazers)
